<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">ะฒัะบันัะฐัะธ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vลญkuลกati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kuลกati</i>. <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะบััะฐัั.html>ะบัฬัะฐัั</a></strong> โข (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kรบลกatสน</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะฟะพะบััะฐัั.html>ะฟะพะบัฬัะฐัั</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ัะบััะฐัั.html>ัะบัฬัะฐัั</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of a guest, woman or child</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to eat, to have <i>(a meal)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Traditionally the word <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะบััะฐัั.html>ะบัฬัะฐัั</a></span> is used in polite invitations to eat when speaking to a woman, a child or especially to a guest. For other occasions the word <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะฑััั.html>ะตััั</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jestสน</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is used. In colloquial speech, however, the word <a href = vnd.unilang:ะบััะฐัั.html>ะบัฬัะฐัั</a> is often used instead of <a href = vnd.unilang:ะฑััั.html>ะตััั</a>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lavร</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะปะฐะฒะบะฐ.html>ะปะฐฬะฒะบะฐ</a></strong> โข (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lรกvka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะปะฐะฒะบะฐ.html>ะปะฐฬะฒะบะธ</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะปะฐะฒะบะฐ.html>ะปะฐฬะฒะบะธ</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะปะฐะฒะบะฐ.html>ะปะฐฬะฒะพะบ</a></b>)
</p>

<li>shop, store</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ะปะฐะดะฐ.html>ะปะฐะด</a> (23636)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ladั</i>, of unknown origin.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะปะฐะดะฐ.html>ะปะฐะด</a></strong> โข (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lad</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะปะฐะดะฐ.html>ะปะฐฬะดะฐ</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะปะฐะดะฐ.html>ะปะฐะดัฬ</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะปะฐะด.html>ะปะฐะดะพฬะฒ</a></b>)
</p>

<li class="senseid" id="Russian-manner,_way">manner, way</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mode; fret</li></ol>
